Babajebaranya i Burundi, n'u Repubulika ya Nazimu (Netherlands) yagendeye umwanzuro, umusore witwa Anna Jochemsen yageze ku ihoro cya giyomwe mu irambi ry'abagize amashyirage b'abagize amashyirage y'imbuga y'igikinyonza (Super-G) ejo. Turamenya kandi ko uburundi, yagendeye umwanzuro, umusore witwa Katja Saarinen yageze ku ihoro cya giyomwe mu irambi ry'abagize amashyirage b'abagize amashyirage y'imbuga y'igikinyonza (Super-G) ejo.
Mitchell Gourley wa wahejeje nk'umwe n'girejeje mu myarere y'abagabo mu myarere ya Super-G y'imbuga. Umusore wa Czech, Oldrich Jelinek, yajejeje nk'umwe n'girejeje ku myarere y'abagabo bagambye mu myarere ya Super-G.
Arly Velasquez wo Mexico yagiyeje nyuma y'umunani mu myinzani y'abagabo mu iruhare rya Super-G. Adam Hall wo ku Misurandi yagiyeje nyuma y'umunyamabanga mu myinzani y'abagabo mu iruhare rya Super-G.
Maciej Krezel, skier wa mwezi w'agatsubasso wa Poland na Anna Ogarzynska (umufashabahari we) bageze i gikombe c'umwaha cya Super-G, bakura i gihankanye na kumbiri. Jong Seork Park wa Korea y'Igihugu yageze i gikombe c'umwaha cya Super-G kuri abagize amashyirage, akura i kijambere cya kumbiri.

Ibyijo bikora umuryo umusangano w'uburasabukire guhuzaho bikwiriye kuba bimwe mu bintu bishoboka nk'icyo gikora amategeko, imitekereze, imagambo, politiki, imaze, gishatira, cyangwa se ukumanika kw'ibi byose.
Abahiri b'umatsiko atari mububaka bagende bakoresha imwe n'imwe mu ndangano zitandukanye z'uko baba bari bagira, zimwe zikora amategeko, uko bagenda, n'imibanozo yabo.
Imwe mu ndemejäro zishobya kusezeranya ubwimbe bw’ukubandika abantu ni ukuvuga ibijyanye n’ibihangano bibaruremye by’abana bari bamaze amavuka ntibamwezeye mu gusanganiwe n’abantu bagendenye nabo mu gihe cyo bari mu myohe.
Abashya abana buriho bitätwa "baturiye" cyangwa se banyamatsiko. Abana batari bamenye amategeko bararimo kubivugwa n’abantu (benshore ari abazabo); mu gihe hariho n’ibijyana by’uko ababona bari bamaze guseka ibyo umwana yari afite mu mpwaro cyangwa se mu koze.
Abashya b’umwana b’imfura bwarashobora kuba bararaye amarasoro make cyangwa se bagasukurirwa n’ibihangano mbere y’uko baparamwa cyangwa se bagenda.
Bwaheze b'imbwa n'ibihando baravugwa ko byarinduwe n'ibyanama; abandi baravugwa ko bari baturutse mu kiruhurura byo byo.
Umuto wari wimwe mu ntara y’ibihangano, akaba yimwe mu batarambika, umwana atera isengesho (mu mpangaca y’ibihangano) akora ibintu byinshi bikomeye nk’ibyo umusubiza, nka gutandika kwibuka abantu cyangwa se kubimenya.

Abana bangeka mu buryo bw’uko baba bagererwa mu buzima bw’ibanga, kubera imabanga bishobora kuba ariyo kubihindura mu by’uko batangwa amatekerezo atandukanye, bishobora kuba ari ukwatswe, gufungwa, cyangwa se kwapfurwa.
Kuri nk'uko umwana wese yateka, ntari kuba yateka mu mfumo itari iyateka, itagira ibyishimo, n’ibishushushwa by’improdamago, ariko ibyo bibaye.

Kuri, ibanza bimwe by'amagenza, cyane cyane amagenza yo mu Bubaruka, bifite imbarage z'ihangano zishobora gutuma amagabi y'ibanza asagara ku magenza raba umusore wari arenda, iyo yari yagenewe gutora inyuma.
Cochamó Valley - Izone ya kuzuza ya Chile, itoriweko nk'iyo Yosemite ya Amerika y'夷ganda, ikaba inyori y'ibihangano bigiye gukura muri granite n'ibihangano by'inyoni.
Isummiti zirimo amagambo mashene y'umwenzura yo ku mabere. Abanyamahirwe bakirura ku bice byose by'ibihangano bakomeka gushakisha izikurikiro zishya mu bubatse bwayo burenze.
Urugusukuramo n'ibihangano by'umw'ishimo, byarimo ukuruka mu kinyarwanda n'ukorera ikinyarwanda, bikaba ingarangezwa mu bintu by'ishimo byo gukora byanduye ku muraru ufite amabaga, ukoresha imirimo y'icyo gihe cyo cy'umutekano cyangwa se umusanso w'icyo gihe cyo cy'umutekano w'icyo gihe cyo cy'umutekano.
Kugenda ku icyo bavuga (skiing) ni umuvuzo mutagabirwa mu bataruka, watumiye abashaka benshi, bakunda gupeza izabukurire byose ku gusukuza mu matahati atari umwe.
Itegeko ry'uko gutamira ni rishatse cyane — imicuro y'ibihangano by'abashijije imizoga yashyizwe muri 5000 BC!
Kugenda mu ski mu bantu nk'ikinyamuzabuka kwateye igihe cyari mu gihe cy'umvigiriko vy'ije, kandi mu 1861 Abanyarwanda baje ku Australia bari bamaze gutangira gusaba umusaba wa ski mu kinyamakuru.
Kugenda mu mutaana mu gisikeli: Ibi bikorwa bikora nshaka bikava nozawekana nka backcountry ski, ski touring, cyangwa se gutambula mu mutaana mu gisikeli.

Sonso ngo irimo kuganama umwese uraruka nka umwese wari yishe.
Mu bijamwaho, uzagera ku kumara za kure kuruta gutwara rimwe riri – ariko rimwe riranduye, utazagera ku kinyamuzabuka kykoyiserezwa cyane nk'umwanzuro mu myohe ya gihatira atari afite ikibanza kirembwe.
Uburanda ni uruf kuri rurafite ukamaro kuruta urundi, ariko rufite igihugu cyinshi gifashwe. Mu bikorwa bish tranquille, gufuka igihugu benshi byavuga ko byashobora kwifotora ku mpapiri z'iviza n'ukwihangana kuri sipiri zitandukanye.
Senzoni za Schengen, muritse, zikivuga nk'igihugu kimwe mu bubusharanvu buri usobora.
Imana ikaba uko usaba, iyo uri muri iyi zone, ushobora kunyura mu misoro atariyo ukava mu kurerwa kwa impapiri z'ikasse.
Nga nahenda, kugira ngo ugende mu bika by’Uburundi bishimye (Schengen), nturi kugira ngo usabe visa kuri buri gihugu cy’umujyanye mu bika bishimye, ibyo bikugabisha igihe, amari na amategeko y’imibaga.
Ariho uburengera bw'umutekano bwarimo kwerekana uko ibyazwe bikora. Iby'imiryango y'ibiziertsi bibona ibintu byo gukora byo byavugwa.
Urugufundure ruri rufaswe n'impamvu z'igicuruzamu
Imikuratezo y’imikophenyli yaba ishobora kuvuzwa nka zimwe mu nkumi, ariko zishya ko gato ku kiyumo cy’imikophenyli y’ububaze.
Uruna ya kutuma isangi itariho ikamere mu buzima bw'abashí Sami, n'imaze yose y'imikoreshwa y'iyi myo itariho ikamere iratekerwa n'abana bakora amabuga asoza.
Nga navumaka, nashaka, abashumi bose b'iSámi batarikiye mu bikuriro bikicururwa by'ishyimbo by'imvuturamo, ariko bampfuye ku cyanga, gusumba n'ibihangano by'imwe n'imbiri, bakoresha amavuka yo gushyushyisha amabuga ariko.
Muzeho haba abantu b'Usaami barafatanya mu batunde b'ibiwo. Kuri Sápmi, ububilityari buri kizamunda bw'ishuri bw'imikungarire.
Nshobora guterekera ko ijambo "Gypsy" rirumiwe cyane, harimo abataratagile bakora urubyiruko, ariko rishobora kuba rikuricirwa kenshi kubisukuramo amatsindo yihariye n’imitekereze ebitandukanye y’abatagize amatsiko yo kuri Abanyarwanda.
Muraho, niba igihugu ushaka kugana kitari mu kiyoboro cy'ihangano, ubuzima bwawe mu gihe cy'urugendo cyangwa se amashyiringi ya trip cancellation yaba yagize impatna.
Ushobora kandi ukomeza gufata amaronzo yo kubona amategeko y'ibihugu bishobora kuba bitandukana na keno kwako, ariko amategeko ayo ariyo yatanzwe abaturage b'icyo gihugu.
Mu bikere biri, abaturage b'Amerika mu Kirahari bari bakwiriye gukora imibereho irangiye n'abaturage b'Uburusiya n'Abanyarwanda.
Amakuru ya kigama niwo kumenyure kitemye kuri ubuzima bw’imigambi mu bw’igihugu kimwe.
Imbonerano ziri zitangazwa zishoborana n'uko zibona, zitari zitafitiye amakuru mashakashake akarihije nk'amakuru y'inshuro atari yishushe.
Uruguguru rurambye ni ibisuzanye byose by’amahirwe yo kuba hari ibيًاko bishobora gufasha, gutera amatsubururwa agabya, cyangwa se gutera amatsva y’abantu.
Urugugushimye rwaikiriza rwimuka mu misozi yose y'isi, rwarimo ibihindutso byinshi, bibaye biri ku mpame, umutagaro, n'imwisuso w'ikirere.
Uruguga rwose, amaso ya kirere, amvugururira cyane, n’ibihango by’urudato ni ingeso n’akamwe k’ihabari ry’umwimbe mutekane, nk’uko ibihangano by’uruguru, amagabi, imirambo y’agati, n’imifuli y’agasiro ni bwo.
Imihurizo rya kijyanye n'ijo serwa rya gihe n'igihugu, nka amatsuba, amasengesho y'icyovu, amatsuba y'ihangi, n'amatsuba y'imbere y'amabuye.

Abantu b'inyarwanda b'inyambishembwe mbere y'amabuga bagomba kutereka amatsiko yabo n'umutekano wabo atari amaze kumenywa igihe bagasukurwa n'ibuga.
Amakuru ya amakara yo gukura ariyo kantu gishatira mu maze y'ibiherekeza bitaruka ku biperi by'ibiherekeza byo ku guti, heme mu kivu cy'ihirwe cyangwa inyoni y'uko.

Kuguruka nk'ibihereke by'ihirwe, byo bije bishimwa n'abantu, byari umuzuro mu ndangano ya Isi ya Japan witsinda umyaka ya 8.
Itegeko rishatse muri Qinā, aho ibiburi byagutse byari umusaraba.
Mu Japan, urwendo rwa mbere rw'ibihangano by'ibiherekezo rwatemo kwa ubutegeko gusa kuri we n'abagenSpare mu banda by'Inkombe ya Gitutu.

Rezura ko itwara rya bus waba ut soovye riga Hebron, ntabwo riga isenguruko mu Ndagurembwa ya Abayuda ya Kiryat Arba gusa.
Amakuru y'inyama ya gikombe yaba icumenye nk'uyuhefuro ukwihangana kw'urugendo.
Kuvuga ngo kumenya, kutora kwa urubuga rwa zamuka mu bihugu byo muri France nka mu nharo ya Loire, mu nharo ya Rhine, cyangwa se gutora kwa irubuga rya kuri umutamu wa Danube, cyangwa se gutora mu majyaru ya Erie.
Babihinde bakana imihirwe y'amabaha n'amagurane y'imigati n'amabaha y'ukuri.
Isumo rye Igisenyi ni rimwe mu ndagushimye zikomeye zo mu Itagatifa Iseru, kandi rikiri mu ngero nk’itaruka ry’Indagushimye Yesu.
Bimwe myo itandukanye by’imigenderi y’uyu mushinga wa uruganda byaragenyekanye n’abantu b’ibihangano b’Igihirwe mu bigihugu by’Abazebenza n’abantu b’ibanjiro mu bimaze ingabo by’imidazole.
